<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:завысить.html>завы́сить</a> (18898)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-вы́сить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-výsitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завысить.html>завы́сить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zavýsitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">завыша́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to overstate, to overrate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:завысить.html>завы́сить</a></b> кому́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:оценка.html>оце́нку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zavýsitʹ</b> komú-libo océnku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give someone an overrated mark/grade</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:завысить.html>завы́сить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:цена.html>це́ны</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:товар.html>това́ры</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zavýsitʹ</b> cény na továry</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to overprice goods</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:завысить.html>завы́сить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:расход.html>расхо́ды</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zavýsitʹ</b> rasxódy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to overstate expenditures (in a budget, etc.)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высокий.html>высо́кий</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vysókij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выше.html>вы́ше</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">výše</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высочайший.html>высоча́йший</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vysočájšij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высокий.html>высоко́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vysokó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высокий.html>высо́ко</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vysóko</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:завышенный.html>завы́шенный</a> (18898)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***завязать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:завязать.html>завяза́ть</a> (5299)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вязать.html>вяза́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vjazátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завязать.html>завяза́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zavjazátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завязывать.html>завя́зывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to tie up, to fasten</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to start, to strike up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:завязать.html>завяза́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:знакомство.html>знако́мство</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zavjazátʹ</b> znakómstvo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to strike up an acquaintance</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to quit (a bad habit or activity)</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завязать.html>завяза́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zavjazátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завязнуть.html>завя́знуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stick <i>(in)</i>, to sink <i>(in)</i></li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завязать.html>завяза́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zavjazátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завязаться.html>завяза́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zavjazátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завязываться.html>завя́зываться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to be/get tied up [tied into a knot]</li>
<li>to set in, to begin, to start
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:завязаться.html>завяза́лся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:разговор.html>разгово́р</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zavjazálsja</b> razgovór</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a conversation began</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:завязаться.html>завяза́лась</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:оживленный.html>оживлённая</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:переписка.html>перепи́ска</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:между.html>ме́жду</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zavjazálasʹ</b> oživljónnaja perepíska (méždu)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a lively correspondence sprang up (between)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(fruit)</i> to set</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завязать.html>завяза́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zavjazátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вязнуть.html>вя́знуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vjáznutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завязнуть.html>завя́знуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zavjáznutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вязнуть.html>вя́знуть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завязать.html>завяза́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stick <i>(in)</i>, to sink <i>(in)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:завязнуть.html>завя́знуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:грязь.html>гря́зи</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zavjáznutʹ</b> v grjázi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to stick in the mud</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to get stuck <i>(in)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:завязнуть.html>завя́знуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:долг.html>долга́х</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zavjáznutʹ</b> v dolgáx</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be up to one's neck in debt</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***завязываться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:завязываться.html>завя́зываться</a> (25893)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завязывать.html>завя́зывать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zavjázyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завязываться.html>завя́зываться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zavjázyvatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завязаться.html>завяза́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to be/get tied up <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">tied into a knot</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to set in, to begin, to start</li>
<li><i>(fruit)</i> to set</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:загадать.html>загада́ть</a> (22131)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гадать.html>гада́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gadátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загадать.html>загада́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zagadátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загадывать.html>зага́дывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><i>(riddle)</i> to set, to offer
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:загадать.html>загада́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:загадка.html>зага́дку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zagadátʹ</b> zagádku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to ask a riddle</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to think <i>(of)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:загадать.html>загада́йте</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:число.html>число́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zagadájte</b> čisló</i> ― <span class="e-translation">think of a number</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make plans, to plan ahead</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:загадочный.html>зага́дочный</a> (3200)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загадка.html>зага́дка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zagádka</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">riddle, enigma</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гадать.html>гада́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gadátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to divine, to foretell</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загадочный.html>зага́дочный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zagádočnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>enigmatic, mysterious</li>
<li>obscure <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">difficult to understand</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>riddlesome</li></ol>

***загадывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:загадывать.html>зага́дывать</a> (20477)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загадать.html>загада́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zagadátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загадывать.html>зага́дывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zagádyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загадать.html>загада́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><i>(riddle)</i> to set, to offer
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:загадывать.html>зага́дывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:загадка.html>зага́дки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zagádyvatʹ</b> zagádki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to ask riddles</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to think <i>(of)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загадать.html>загада́йте</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:число.html>число́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zagadájte čisló</i> ― <span class="e-translation">think of a number</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make plans, to plan ahead
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:загадывать.html>зага́дывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:будущее.html>бу́дущее</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zagádyvatʹ</b> na búduščeje</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to try to predict events; guess at the future</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бу́дем</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:загадывать.html>зага́дывать</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne búdem <b>zagádyvatʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">let's not make plans too early</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:загар.html>зага́р</a> (10049)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загар.html>зага́р</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zagár</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загар.html>зага́ра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загар.html>зага́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загар.html>зага́ров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>suntan, tan (darkened coloration of the skin)</li></ol>

***загибать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:загибать.html>загиба́ть</a> (16162)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-гиба́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-gibátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загибать.html>загиба́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zagibátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загнуть.html>загну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to turn up, to turn down, to bend
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:загибать.html>загиба́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:палец.html>па́лец</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zagibátʹ</b> pálec</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bend/crook a finger</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:загибать.html>загиба́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:палец.html>па́льцы</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:счет.html>счёте</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zagibátʹ</b> pálʹcy (pri sčóte)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to count off on one's fingers</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:загибать.html>загиба́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:страница.html>страни́цу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zagibátʹ</b> stranícu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">turn down [dog-ear] the page</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:загибать.html>загиба́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:цена.html>це́ну</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zagibátʹ</b> cénu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to ask/charge an exorbitant price</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to exaggerate, to pull someone's leg</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> usually perfective</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to say, to let loose</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:загибаться.html>загиба́ться</a> (19204)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загибать.html>загиба́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zagibátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загибаться.html>загиба́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zagibátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загнуться.html>загну́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to curl up; to curl down <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of the edge of something</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to bend</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to kick the bucket, to bite the dust, to croak, to die</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загибать.html>загиба́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zagibátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
